 Finance Minister Arun Jaitley wrote a blog after the imposition of President's rule
 jisaki pehali panktiyon main se ek pankti yah thi ki raashtrapati shashan lagane kaa faisalaa raashtrapati ne apni raajnneetik samajhadaari or apane saare rakhe gaye dastavezon ke aadhaar par liya
 The same argument was given by the lawyer of the Central Government in the High Court
 hoicourt ne kah diya ki People can take wrong decisions, whether they are president or judge
 
 
 ye koi raja kaa faisalaa nahin he, jisaki nyaayik samiksha naa ho sakati ho
 The central government strongly defended its decision in the name of the President's approval, while the proposal is passed by the Union Cabinet
 raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ek baar vichaar ke liye bhej sakate the
 Which they did not send
 ek baar bhi sawaal nahin kiya
 If the proposal comes again from the cabinet, they would have to say yes
 sawaal yah uth rahaa he ki unhone dobaaraa vichaar ke liye kyon nahin bheja
 Nevertheless, the central government continued to argue in the court and channels outside the court that the President had seen the documents
 uttarakhand hoicourt kaa faisla is maamle main aitihaasik he ki usne centre sarkaar ke us kendriya tark ko hi dharashayi kar diya jiske sahare raashtrapati shashan kaa bachaav kiya ja rahaa tha
 'this is not the decision of a king, who cannot have a judicial review
 ' ye pankti aane vaale samay main bhartiya loktantr ke raajnneetik itihaas main jamaane tak guunjegi
 Whenever a President signs the proposal of imposing President's rule, he will remember it once
 unke salaahkaar yaad dilaayenge
 You are not the king
 aap jo faisla le rahe hai uski adaalat main samiksha ho sakati he
 The Leader of the Opposition and all those who know the Constitution are also questioning the President
 public main aakar raashtrapati apana bachaav nahin kar sakate magar public to sawaal karegi
 The role of the governor, not only the president, should also be reviewed
 uttarakhand hoicourt ne rajyapal ke bare main bhi kaha ki wo nishpaksh hota he
 There is no central agent
 aap samvidhan ke jaankaar or supreme court ke senior edwocket raju ramchandran hai
 He has also been an advisor to the Supreme Court in many cases
 raju ramchandran kaa kahana he ki is puure maamle main raashtrapati kii bhoomika se niraash hai
 The President should have exercised his discretionary powers
 is maamle main unki bhoomika bhale hi simit ho
 He had asked questions in the case of President's rule in Arunachal Pradesh, but in Uttarakhand, he did not raise any questions while the floor test was about to take place
 aap vaajapeyi sarkaar main atorni general rahe soli psorabji hai
 Eminent constitutionalist Sorabji said that the Modi government should not have been hasty in the matter of imposing President's rule in Uttarakhand
 isse ye sandesh gaya ki centre sarkaar flor test nahin hone dena chaahati
 Sorabji is not as strict as Ramachandran, but said that one could say that the President should have sent the file back to the government, but what if the government had sent the file back
 raashtrapati ko dastakhat karne padate
 
 
 The President did nothing wrong
 
 
 court ab active hai isliye sarkaar ko saavdhaanee se kaam karnaa chahie tha
 In 1994, a 9-judge bench of the Supreme Court ruled in the SR Bommai case that Article 356 should be used to impose President's rule only in very specific circumstances
 centre sarkaar ke raajnneetik hit ke liye kabhi nahin hona chahie
 The Uttarakhand High Court gave its verdict in less than a month
 apane aap main itihaas he
 They have given the decision even during the old government
 aisa nahin ki duusari sarkaar ban gai yaa chunaav hokar koi or sarkaar aa gai phir faisla aayaa
 Therefore, the decision of Uttarakhand High Court and later the decision of the Supreme Court will now be taught
 par iske liye karnataka ke purv mukhyamantri es aar bommai kaa shukraguzaar hona chahie jo apni sarkaar kii barkhaastagi ke liye adalati ladaai lade
 It is another matter that he did not get the benefit of this fight
 jab supreme court kaa faisla aayaa tab unki sarkaar ja chuki thi
 Then Bommai's government was sacked by the Congress government at the Center
 aaj congress ko bommai kii us ladaai se laabh hua he
 Harish Rawat's government has survived
 magar is ladaai main harish ravat ne bhi jod diya
 What an irony raashtrapati shashan ke maamle main congress naitik rup se kisi bahes main tik nahin paati he lekin usne uttarakhand ke bahaane aisi bahason ke liye naitik bal hasil kar liya he
 Harish Rawat also became part of constitutional history in this case
 rahul gandhi ne kaha ki wo galat kar rahe the
 We were doing it right
 loktantr kii jeet hui he
 President's rule was imposed in Arunachal Pradesh on 26 January this year
 congress ne ise bhi chunauti di magar supreme court kii samvidhan peeth main sunwaayee chalati rahi or arunachal pradesh main nai sarkaar ban gai
 The final decision of the Supreme Court has not yet come
 hamane raashtrapati shashan ke bare main desh ke kanoon mantri sadanand gauda ke bayaan ko google main khub search kiya
 i may not have received it, so i am not saying the claim, but except the Law Minister, the statements of all the leaders must be received
 kya ye ajeeb nahin he ki itani badi sanvaidhanik bahes ho gai or kanoon mantri kaa ek twit tak nahin he
 Was this case political? sadanand gauda ne buudhvaar ko supreme court kaa faisla aane ke baad soyal health card or beti bachaao beti padhaao par twit kiya he
 Finance Minister Arun Jaitley's blog found
 jise unhone hindi or angreji main likhaa tha
 Uttarakhand High Court Chief Justice KM Joseph and Justice VK Bisht had said during the hearing that the central government should be fair in the matter of President's rule in Uttarakhand but it is behaving like a private party
 ham aahat hai ki centre sarkaar aisa vyavhaar kar rahi he
 How can you think of playing such a game with the court
 chif justise ke em joseph kaa ab tabadalaa ho chukaa he
 But his bench has set a scale in terms of President's rule
 supreme court kaa faisla bhi usee disha main rahaa he
 This decision has given a new lease of life to Harish Rawat, who is surrounded by many allegations and his opponents within the party
 tippaniyan For Harish Rawat, it turned out to be a political battle in which he caught the efforts of the Modi government and his political opponents in the party in one blow
 purv mukhyamantri vijay bahuguna or purv mantri harak singh ravat ke saath nau vidhayak naa idhar ke rahe, naa udhar ke
 On the basis of these rebels of the Congress, the BJP had planned to defeat the Harish Rawat government in the state
 baagiyon ne harish ravat sarkaar ko barkhaast karne ke liye rajyapal ko die khat main bijepi ke letters pad par hastakshar kiye
 He flew from Dehradun to Delhi with BJP leaders and rode in buses with BJP leaders to Gurgaon and sometimes to Jaipur
 five star hotalon main tehre
 In Delhi, he issued a sting against Harish Rawat and also accused him of corruption, but nothing worked
 vidhansabha main bhi haar kaa munh dekhnaa padaa or uttarakhand hycourt main bhi
 The Uttarakhand High Court rejected the petition of these rebels and ratified the Speaker's decision to cancel their legislative assembly
 hycourt ne kaha ki un vidhayakon ne apane kaam se khud hi raajnneetik dal se apni sadsyta chhod dene kaa kaam kiya he
 Now there are very few options left in front of these rebels
 kai ke siyaasi kariyar sankat main pad gaye hai
 Neither does he make a comeback in Congress, nor does he join BJP
 harish ravat kii jeet ke baad bijepi ke liye bhi unki koi khaas ahmiyat nahin rah gai he
 Nawaz Sharif was reinstated in Pakistan by the Supreme Court in 1993
 jise raashtrapati ghulaam ishaq khan ne barkhaast kar diya tha
 It was the first government in both countries that was reinstated after the president's dismissal
 faisale ke baad nawaz sharif ke ek mantri ne kaha tha ki na khuda hi mila na visaale sanam, na idhar ke rahe na udhar ke rahe
 March 18 to May 11 arrived
 uttarakhand jahaan se chalaa tha vahiin pahunch gaya
 Due to this Uttarakhand, it was so long that Samajwadi Party MP Jaya Bachchan got annoyed in Rajya Sabha one day
 unhone kaha ki uttarakhand ke kaaran kai zaruri masalon par charchaa nahin ho rahi he
 Harish Rawat does not have to take oath again
 adaalat kaa aadesh aate hi kendriya mantrimandal kii baithak hui or raashtrapati shashan hataane kaa faisalaa kar liya gaya
 The BJP tried to justify President's rule at all levels on the basis of allegations of constitutionalism, morality and corruption, but the BJP, which gave the slogan of collaborative federalism, could not prove its point in the court
 ek maheene se zyada samay tak ek chuni hui sarkaar ko barkhaast tak kai staron par saarvajanik bahason ke zariye vakt bhi barbaad hui
 a case of sting operation came up twice, in which Rawat was also accused of attempting to save the government from money
 sting oparation se jo sawaal uthe or raashtrapati shashan lagane ko lekar jo sawaal uth rahe the, donon kaa koi sambandh nahin tha
 But the BJP continued to make every effort to defend President's rule through a sting operation
 mashhoor vakil harish salve ne jab sting oparation kaa hawala diya to uttarakhand hoicourt ne kaha ki agar raashtrapati bhrashtachar ke aaropon ke aadhaar par rajyon main apana shashan thopane lagenge to koi rajya sarkaar paanch minute se zyada nahin chal paaegi
 However, the CBI is also investigating the case of sting operation
 sab kuch tezi se hua magar gum phir kar ravat ke darvaaze pahunch gaya
 He is now Chief Minister again

 The government said that any citizen can visit the nearest Indian Embassy or High Commission and apply for an Emergency Certificate for repatriation
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa vikaas swaroop ne kaha ki apatkaaleen praaanpatr vishesh rup se kisi bhartiya naagarik ko bharat lautne ke lihaaj se uplabdh yatra dastavej he or maalya ko yah suvidha uplabdh he
 Mallya told a Delhi court that he wanted to come to India but was unable to return due to the passport being suspended
 is bare main puche jane par swaroop ne kaha, ‘hamaari sthiti bahut spasht he
 Any Indian citizen who resides outside India and who does not have any valid travel documents for any reason, will only have to come to the nearest Indian Embassy or High Commission and apply for an emergency certificate
 ’ Mallya is currently in London
 unhone pheraa ulanghan ke ek maamle ke silsile main kathith taur par sammanon kii avhelnaa karne ke liye darj maamle main mukhya metropolitan magistrate ke samaksh apane vakil ke madhyam daleel di thi

 kisi ko nahin mila bahumatadrasal manipur main kisi bhi party ko bahumat nahin mila he

 congress 28 siten jitkar sabase badi party bani he

 aise main koi bhi party bahumat yani 31 siton kaa jaadui aankada nahin chhu pai he

 jharkhand main sirf ek rupee main hoti he mahilaon ke naam registriab tak dedh lakh mahilaayein baniin jameen or makaan kii malkinjharkhand desh kaa pehla rajya he, jahaan par sirf ek rupee main hi mahilaayein sampatti kii malkin ban jaati hai
 Since the facility started two years ago, one and a half lakh women have availed the scheme so far
 desh ke baaki rajyon main bhi mahilaon ko registy main kuch pratishat kii chhot jarur milti he, magar kahin par bhi ek rupee main hi jameen yaa makaan kii registry kii suvidha nahin he
 In Delhi, women have to pay four percent stamp duty, while in UP only one percent is exempted from stamp duty
 jharkhand main amuman chah se saat pratishat registry shulk chukaana padataa he
 In such a situation, all the families are saving huge stamp duty by registering the names of women
 mukhyamantri raghubar das ne guuruuvaar ko twit kar is yojana kaa laabh uthaane vaali dedh lakh mahilaon kaa aankada diya
 He tweeted, "jharkhand is the first state in the country where the registry of land / house up to Rs 50 lakh for women is done in just one rupee
 ab tak dedh lakh se zyada mahilaayein ban chuki hai makaan malkin
 "actually, Prime Minister Narendra Modi appealed for a registry of home land in the name of women for women's empowerment
 jiske baad 2017 main jharkhand cabinet ne sirf ek rupee main mahilaon ko registry suvidha dene kaa faisla kiya
 According to this, to take advantage of this exemption, a woman has to file an affidavit that she is taking advantage of such exemption for the first time
 niyam ke mutabik ek rupee main registry kaa laabh koi mahila ek baar hi le sakati he
 There will be no exemption on registration with the man
 vahiin agar do mahilaayein sanyukt rup se sampatti kii registry karaati hai to unhen laabh milegaa
 However, if the property is worth more than 50 lakhs, women will have to pay stamp duty on the additional amount
 jharkhand desh kaa pehla rajya he jahaan mahilaon ke liye 50 lakh rupee tak kii jameen / makaan kii registry sirf ek rupee main hoti he
 So far, more than one and a half lakh women have become landlords
 kaam kiya he

 yahaan raashtrapati keaar narayanan or pradhanmantri atal bihari vaajapeyi ne unka hero jaisaa swaagat kiya
 The comments zyaadaatar logon ke liye ye anubhav kaam chhodane ke liye kaaphi hota, lekin nachiketa alag hi mitti ke bane the
 Due to a back injury sustained during the ejection in Kargil, he could not return to the forward plane
 haalanki nachi, jaisaa ki dost unhen pukaarte hai, bhartiya vayusena ke transport flit main shaamil hue or vishaal Il-76 trassport vimaan udaate hai
 Nachchi, 17 years after Kargil, says, 'the heart of a pilot is always in the cockpit

 i reached the ground fairly soon
 vah bahut neeche se kiya gaya ijection tha
 The white sheet of snow was spread everywhere around where i landed
 us jagah par goliyaan baras rahi thi, jisase ijection ke jatke ke baad mujhe turant hosh aayaa or meraa aglaa lakshya khud ko cover karnaa tha
 ' iske kareeb aadhe ghante baad pakistani sainikon ne un par ghaat lagaakar hamalaa kiya, haalanki isse pehle nachiketa un par goliyon kii apni magazine khaali kar chuke the
 He says, 'we keep a small pistol for protection
 main dekh saktaa tha ki jahaan maine cover le rakhaa tha, vahaan paanch-chah log (mujh par) ghaat lagaae hai
 i fired the first shot
 or iske baad maine unhen rokane kii koshish main sari goliyaan daag di, taaki vah mere paas nahin aaen
 Unfortunately, our pistol range was just 25 yards, while they had AK-56
 isliye, pakkaa tha ki unki goliyaan to mujh par baras rahi hai, lekin meri goliyaan un tak nahin pahunch paa raheen or isse pehle kii main duusari magazine bharta, vah aae or mujhe bandhak bana liya
 ' nachiketa ko bandhak banane vaale pakistan ke nardan lite inphantry ke sainik behad krur the or unhen tab buree tarah peetate rahe, jab unke ek varisht adhikari ne unhen peeche hatane ko nahin kaha
 Nachiketa says, "the men holding me were banging with me and perhaps they intended to kill me, because for them i was just an enemy pilot firing bullets from the sky at their hideout
" khushkismati se, vahaan aayaa adhikari behad maior tha
 He understood the situation that i am now his hostage and now i do not need to be treated like that
 to unase un logon ko roka, jisamen kaaphi koshish lagi, lekin ve log us vakt kaaphi ugr the
 'nachiketa's picture a day before Pakistan was taken hostage nachiketa ko phir pakistan ke kabje vaale kashmir le jaaya gaya, antarrashtriya media ke saamne khadaa kiya gaya or phir soochnaaon ke liye maaraa-peeta gaya
 However, Nachiketa had no idea of the efforts being made for his release
 vah kehete hai, 'poochtacha shuru ho chuki thi or mujhe pataa tha ki shaayad main kal naa dekh paaun
